So, following the standard ICD of 3 hits/2.5s, that&#8217;s: (I = hydro application, O = no application)<br> 1st NA: IO + orbital (NA+CA vape)<br> 2nd NA: OIO (CA vape)<br> 3rd NA: OIOOI (CA vape + blossom vape)<br> 4th NA: IO + orbital &lt;= 2.5s refresh (NA+CA vape)<br> 5th NA: OIO (CA vape)<br> 6th NA: OIOOI (CA vape)</p><p>With yelan (taken from beta test result) it usually goes like this:<br> 1st NA: IOO (NA+CA vape)<br> 2nd NA: IOO (CA vape)<br> 3rd NA: IOO (CA vape, blossom apply pyro aura)<br> 4th NA: IOO (yelan forward vape, hutao perform 3NA, 1st NA apply pyro aura)<br> 5th NA: IOO (yelan forward vape)<br> 6th NA: IOO (yelan apply hydro, hutao CA vape)</p><p>Legends: NA = normal attack, CA = charged attack<br> 3NA = 3 normal attack strings</p><p>See the main difference? With xinqiu, hutao can infinitely perform 1NA-CA-jump/dash cancel combo and will reverse vape all of her CA. With yelan, hutao need to do 3x 1NA-CA followed by 3NA-CA then repeat to allow her to reverse vape all of her CA. Doable, but a huge pain in the arse. Do keep in mind that the 3NA-CA hutao does must be delayed to accommodate for yelan&#8217;s proc CD, which is another layer of pain.<br> With zhongli in the team, you&#8217;ll need to run away before creating any pillar. With albedo in the team, good luck.<br> So, demand buff, don&#8217;t overhype. We want yelan strong, not clunky. Thank you for your attention.</p></div></div></div> </li> <li id=comment-87882 class="comment even thread-even depth-1 comment"><div class=row><div class="comment-wrap col-md-12"><ul
